# Dashboard PRD Plan: Roko And Chain Additions

**Source:** `/Users/will/dev/nunchi/nunchi-dashboard/docs/prd/21-roko-and-chain-additions.md`
**Generated:** 2026-04-25
**Source hash:** `c1af2705c85857ea13213ef4c00c5394301018f5dd2792ebe1cf468c54fcdf0b`
**Section tasks:** 49
**Context mode:** full source section embedded in every task; no excerpt truncation.
**Quality threshold:** every task must score at least 9.5/10 before implementation begins.

## Purpose
Turn every dashboard PRD section into explicit backend-support work. Even visual/frontend sections must produce backend projection, telemetry, fixture, schema, or explicit no-backend rationale so frontend implementation is easy and stable.

## Global Implementation Rules
- Extend existing modules before creating new ones; only add new route/service files when no canonical owner exists.
- Implement production wiring, not only structs, mocks, or isolated helpers.
- Preserve every extracted detail unless a parity-ledger row explicitly marks it covered or deferred.
- Add persistence, events, auth/safety, dashboard projections, and docs updates whenever the requirement reaches those surfaces.
- A checked box means code, tests, docs, parity ledger, and strict gates are done for that task.

## Primary Target Areas
- `crates/roko-serve/src/routes/chain.rs`
- `crates/roko-chain/src/`
- `apps/mirage-rs/src/`

### DASH-21-S001 -- 21 — Roko and chain additions

**Source section:** `/Users/will/dev/nunchi/nunchi-dashboard/docs/prd/21-roko-and-chain-additions.md:1` through `14`
**Heading level:** H1

**Implementation status:** `[ ] not started` `[ ] in progress` `[ ] implemented` `[ ] verified`

**Full source context for this task:**

````markdown
# 21 — Roko and chain additions

*What the Nunchi dashboard needs from Roko, Korai, Mirage, and smart contracts that does not yet exist. Proposed additions, tagged by necessity.*

> **⚠️ Architecture update (2026-04-24):** The roko architecture docs (`/roko/tmp/architecture/`) and DeFi gap analysis (`/roko/tmp/defi/gap/`) significantly expand the API surface described here. Key changes:
> - **Three-tier deployment model** (backbone/workspace/remote) replaces the single-backend assumption
> - **12 universal primitives** (doc 23) supersede the 10-primitive model — adds Connector, Feed, Recipe
> - **~160 new API endpoints** across 17 categories
> - **DeFi risk/safety UI** with pre-action gates, position tracking, MEV detection
> - **Paid feeds** with x402/MPP micropayment protocols
> - See `docs/plan/architecture-cross-reference.md` for the full mapping.

---
````

**Explicit detail extraction from this section:**

- Section word count: `114`
- Section hash: `776e69a52b774a92fac1f6305bc69ef195171a2f8078071acf43f23d73a184e8`

Key changes: > - **Three-tier deployment model** (backbone/workspace/remote) replaces the single-backend assumption > - **12 universal primitives** (doc 23) supersede the 10-primitive model — adds Connector, Feed, Recipe > - **~160 new API endpoints** across 17 categories > - **DeFi risk/safety UI** with pre-action gates, position tracking, MEV detection > - **Paid feeds** with x402/MPP micropayment protocols > - See `docs/plan/architecture-cross-reference.md` for the full mapping.

**Concern contracts to satisfy:**
- API: define concrete request/response structs, auth scope, error shape, pagination/filtering, idempotency semantics, and generated API-reference/OpenAPI coverage.
- Realtime: emit typed Bus/StateHub events with room, sequence, actor, timestamp, replay/degraded semantics, and dashboard cache-update payload.
- Storage: define deterministic schema, migration/default behavior, corruption handling, restart recovery, cleanup/GC, and fixture data.
- Chain: default to devnet/simulation, prove contract/client/indexer sync, enforce wallet/risk/simulation gates, and record audit/witness data.
- Runtime: wire into the production agent loop with lifecycle, cancellation, health, audit, provider/tool safety, and observable events.
- Frontend support: provide stable projections, mock fixtures, empty/loading/stale/degraded/unauthorized states, and realtime update payloads that match projection schemas.
- Verification: add deterministic unit, integration, route/CLI, auth/safety, persistence/restart, serialization, and failing-path tests; avoid LLM self-grading where ground truth is required.
- Config/deployment: validate defaults, hot reload or restart-required paths, env var diagnostics, service dry-runs, and non-destructive operations.

### DASH-21-S002 -- Why this document matters

**Source section:** `/Users/will/dev/nunchi/nunchi-dashboard/docs/prd/21-roko-and-chain-additions.md:15` through `28`
**Heading level:** H2
**Concern split:** `api`, `realtime`, `storage`, `auth`, `chain`, `agent-runtime`, `dashboard-support`, `verification`
**Implementation status:** `[ ] not started` `[ ] in progress` `[ ] implemented` `[ ] verified`

**Full source context for this task:**

````markdown
## Why this document matters

The dashboard cannot invent backend capabilities it needs. If the Agent Fleet page wants to show per-agent cost aggregates, Roko or a dashboard service must expose that data. If the Arena Constructor wants to publish an arena on-chain, a contract must accept the publication. If the Meta-Lineage view wants to trace objects across generations, the lineage must be recorded somewhere.

This document names what the dashboard specifications from `11-pulse-surfaces.md` through `19-authoring-surfaces.md` assume exists on the backend side, and which of those assumptions require additions that are not yet built. Each addition is tagged by priority:

- **[required]** — the dashboard specification depends on this existing. Without it, the corresponding surface cannot work.
- **[valuable]** — the dashboard works without it, but the user experience improves substantially with it.
- **[speculative]** — an idea worth considering, not a firm dependency.

This document does not specify the backend additions in detail. It names them and says what the dashboard needs from them. The actual designs (data models, contract interfaces, API schemas) are specified in the Roko and Korai documents, not here.

---
````

**Explicit detail extraction from this section:**

- Section word count: `182`
- Section hash: `a394008452b1e53156ad519c12752b8f3db8b2cfb5e4f0ca7a8b65339eea0d04`

**Normative requirements and implementation claims:**
- The dashboard cannot invent backend capabilities it needs. If the Agent Fleet page wants to show per-agent cost aggregates, Roko or a dashboard service must expose that data. If the Arena Constructor wants to publish an arena on-chain, a contract must accept the publication. If the Meta-Lineage view wants to trace objects across generations, the lineage must be recorded somewhere.
- This document names what the dashboard specifications from `11-pulse-surfaces.md` through `19-authoring-surfaces.md` assume exists on the backend side, and which of those assumptions require additions that are not yet built. Each addition is tagged by priority:
- - **[required]** — the dashboard specification depends on this existing. Without it, the corresponding surface cannot work. - **[valuable]** — the dashboard works without it, but the user experience improves substantially with it. - **[speculative]** — an idea worth considering, not a firm dependency.
- This document does not specify the backend additions in detail. It names them and says what the dashboard needs from them. The actual designs (data models, contract interfaces, API schemas) are specified in the Roko and Korai documents, not here.
- ---

### DASH-21-S003 -- Additions to Roko (the agent runtime)

**Source section:** `/Users/will/dev/nunchi/nunchi-dashboard/docs/prd/21-roko-and-chain-additions.md:29` through `32`
**Heading level:** H2
**Concern split:** `api`, `realtime`, `storage`, `chain`, `agent-runtime`, `dashboard-support`, `config-deployment`
**Implementation status:** `[ ] not started` `[ ] in progress` `[ ] implemented` `[ ] verified`

**Full source context for this task:**

````markdown
## Additions to Roko (the agent runtime)

Roko is the Rust toolkit agents run on. The dashboard connects to Roko via HTTP sidecars exposed by each running agent, plus (likely) a dashboard-specific aggregation service that fans out across many agents' sidecars.
````

**Explicit detail extraction from this section:**

- Section word count: `35`
- Section hash: `bff4da66106c88fe13bff76c30ee7673603b33363518abe18eb8e7ef150428be`

**Normative requirements and implementation claims:**
- Roko is the Rust toolkit agents run on. The dashboard connects to Roko via HTTP sidecars exposed by each running agent, plus (likely) a dashboard-specific aggregation service that fans out across many agents' sidecars.

### DASH-21-S004 -- Per-agent sidecar endpoints

**Source section:** `/Users/will/dev/nunchi/nunchi-dashboard/docs/prd/21-roko-and-chain-additions.md:33` through `66`
**Heading level:** H3
**Concern split:** `api`, `realtime`, `storage`, `chain`, `agent-runtime`, `dashboard-support`, `verification`, `config-deployment`
**Implementation status:** `[ ] not started` `[ ] in progress` `[ ] implemented` `[ ] verified`

**Full source context for this task:**

````markdown
### Per-agent sidecar endpoints

Most of these exist or are implied by existing specifications. Confirming for completeness.

**[required]** `GET /agent/status` — agent's current lifecycle state, current cognitive tier, current tick info.

**[required]** `GET /agent/config` — agent's current configuration (domain, extensions, gates, model routing, budget, caveats).

**[required]** `POST /agent/config` — update configuration (subject to caveats).

**[required]** `GET /agent/events?since={sequence}` — event fabric event stream (also available via WebSocket).

**[required]** `WS /agent/events` — WebSocket event subscription.

**[required]** `GET /agent/episodes?limit={n}&before={time}` — recent episodes.

**[required]** `GET /agent/episodes/{id}` — episode detail.

**[required]** `GET /agent/episodes/{id}/workspace` — the cognitive workspace for an episode (for Context Audit).

**[required]** `GET /agent/knowledge?limit={n}&filter={...}` — agent's local knowledge store entries.

**[required]** `POST /agent/message` — send an operator message to the agent.

**[required]** `POST /agent/pause`, `POST /agent/resume`, `POST /agent/stop` — lifecycle controls.

**[required]** `GET /agent/costs?window={w}` — cost data for the agent.

**[valuable]** `GET /agent/somatic-state` — current somatic marker state, for debug and interpretability surfaces.

**[valuable]** `GET /agent/dream-state` — current dream cycle status.

**[valuable]** `GET /agent/section-effectiveness` — per-context-section effectiveness tracking. Needed for Context Audit's deeper analytics.
````

### DASH-21-S005 -- Per-agent streaming

**Source section:** `/Users/will/dev/nunchi/nunchi-dashboard/docs/prd/21-roko-and-chain-additions.md:67` through `74`
**Heading level:** H3
**Concern split:** `api`, `realtime`, `storage`, `chain`, `agent-runtime`, `dashboard-support`, `config-deployment`
**Implementation status:** `[ ] not started` `[ ] in progress` `[ ] implemented` `[ ] verified`

**Full source context for this task:**

````markdown
### Per-agent streaming

**[required]** Event fabric WebSocket multiplexing — the dashboard needs to subscribe to multiple agents' event streams simultaneously. Likely via a dashboard-side aggregation service that multiplexes many sidecars.

**[required]** Subscription resumption with sequence numbers — on disconnect, resume from the last known sequence. Covered in `10-realtime-and-motion.md`.

**[valuable]** Event filtering server-side — the dashboard can request only specific event types rather than the full stream. Reduces bandwidth.
````

**Explicit detail extraction from this section:**

- Section word count: `68`
- Section hash: `5659b02a8eb8ddc0b992e6b886c916314404a335be188c0572c7deb78cc1660c`

- **[required]** Subscription resumption with sequence numbers — on disconnect, resume from the last known sequence. Covered in `10-realtime-and-motion.md`.
- **[valuable]** Event filtering server-side — the dashboard can request only specific event types rather than the full stream. Reduces bandwidth.

### DASH-21-S006 -- Agent lifecycle operations

**Source section:** `/Users/will/dev/nunchi/nunchi-dashboard/docs/prd/21-roko-and-chain-additions.md:75` through `84`
**Heading level:** H3
**Concern split:** `api`, `realtime`, `storage`, `chain`, `agent-runtime`, `dashboard-support`, `config-deployment`
**Implementation status:** `[ ] not started` `[ ] in progress` `[ ] implemented` `[ ] verified`

**Full source context for this task:**

````markdown
### Agent lifecycle operations

**[required]** Deploy an agent — spawn a new Roko runtime with a given configuration. Must work locally, in managed cloud, and against user-provided infrastructure. API: `POST /agents/deploy` with the agent configuration.

**[required]** Terminate an agent — clean shutdown, genome extraction if mortality is opted in. API: `POST /agents/{id}/terminate`.

**[valuable]** Migrate an agent — move a running agent from one runtime to another (e.g., local → cloud). Requires state serialization; currently only partially supported.

**[valuable]** Fork an agent — create a new agent with the same configuration as an existing one, but with fresh identity. Different from template-forking because an actual running agent's state can be captured.
````

**Explicit detail extraction from this section:**

- Section word count: `108`
- Section hash: `f2b0e425fa7d354683fddba83281b96cc5f63841a4541812b52a20f02e6d14f3`

**Normative requirements and implementation claims:**
- **[required]** Deploy an agent — spawn a new Roko runtime with a given configuration. Must work locally, in managed cloud, and against user-provided infrastructure. API: `POST /agents/deploy` with the agent configuration.
- **[required]** Terminate an agent — clean shutdown, genome extraction if mortality is opted in. API: `POST /agents/{id}/terminate`.
- **[valuable]** Migrate an agent — move a running agent from one runtime to another (e.g., local → cloud). Requires state serialization; currently only partially supported.
- **[valuable]** Fork an agent — create a new agent with the same configuration as an existing one, but with fresh identity. Different from template-forking because an actual running agent's state can be captured.

- None extracted from this section.

- None extracted from this section.

- None extracted from this section.

- None extracted from this section.

- local -> cloud

- None extracted from this section.

- None extracted from this section.

- None extracted from this section.

````markdown
### Dashboard aggregation service

**[required]** A service that fans out across many agents' sidecars to produce aggregate views. Responsibilities:

- Aggregate cost across agents.
- Aggregate event streams for Live Console and Event Stream at scale.
- Cross-agent queries (find all agents matching criteria).
- Fleet-level operations (bulk pause, bulk message).

This service does not yet exist in the specified form. It may be a thin HTTP layer, an in-process component of the dashboard backend, or a dedicated microservice.
````

````markdown
### Cross-user queries

**[valuable]** A mechanism for querying other users' public agents. For Network (Fleet section) and Network Pulse. Must respect privacy — only public agents appear; their public state is exposed; their private state is not.

**[valuable]** A mechanism for observing other users' public knowledge. For Knowledge Store in Global Lens.

**[valuable]** A mechanism for cross-user groups — coordination across agents owned by different users.
````

- Chain: default to devnet/simulation, prove contract/client/indexer sync, enforce wallet/risk/simulation gates, and record audit/witness data.

- Config/deployment: validate defaults, hot reload or restart-required paths, env var diagnostics, service dry-runs, and non-destructive operations.

### DASH-21-S011 -- Agent passport registry (ERC-8004)

**Source section:** `/Users/will/dev/nunchi/nunchi-dashboard/docs/prd/21-roko-and-chain-additions.md:114` through `123`
**Heading level:** H3
**Concern split:** `api`, `realtime`, `storage`, `auth`, `chain`, `agent-runtime`, `dashboard-support`, `config-deployment`
**Implementation status:** `[ ] not started` `[ ] in progress` `[ ] implemented` `[ ] verified`

**Full source context for this task:**

````markdown
### Agent passport registry (ERC-8004)

**[required]** An ERC-8004 registry contract. Already specified in the Korai PRDs but worth calling out as the dashboard hard-depends on it.

- `registerAgent(config)` — register a new agent, receive passport.
- `updateAgent(tokenId, config)` — update agent metadata.
- `getAgent(tokenId)` — read agent passport.
- `getAgentsByOwner(address)` — list an owner's agents.
- `getAgentsByCapability(capability)` — discovery by capability.
````

````markdown
### Reputation registry

**[required]** A reputation registry contract tracking per-agent per-domain reputation scores.

- `getReputation(tokenId, domain)` — read current reputation.
- `getReputationHistory(tokenId, domain, range)` — historical scores.
- Update mechanism is restricted to attested sources (arena settlement, clearing outcomes, etc.).
````

### DASH-21-S014 -- Arena registry

**Source section:** `/Users/will/dev/nunchi/nunchi-dashboard/docs/prd/21-roko-and-chain-additions.md:143` through `154`
**Heading level:** H3

**Implementation status:** `[ ] not started` `[ ] in progress` `[ ] implemented` `[ ] verified`

**Full source context for this task:**

````markdown
### Arena registry

**[valuable]** An arena registry contract for discoverability.

- `registerArena(config, stake)` — register a new arena with a daeji stake.
- `getArena(arenaId)` — read.
- `listArenas(filter)` — discovery.
- `submitAttempt(arenaId, attemptData)` — submit.
- `getLeaderboard(arenaId)` — read.

Arenas could exist off-chain initially (arenas as data on a regular HTTP service) and move on-chain as the registry matures. Off-chain MVP is acceptable if bandwidth to implement on-chain isn't available immediately.
````

- Arenas could exist off-chain initially (arenas as data on a regular HTTP service) and move on-chain as the registry matures. Off-chain MVP is acceptable if bandwidth to implement on-chain isn't available immediately.

### DASH-21-S018 -- Pheromone deposits

**Full source context for this task:**

````markdown
### Pheromone deposits

**[required]** A mechanism for depositing pheromones on-chain. Each pheromone has:

- Type.
- Strength.
- Decay rate.
- Source agent.
- Position (HDC fingerprint or semantic position).

Pheromones are publicly readable. Decay is computed deterministically from the on-chain age.
````

````markdown
### Delegation caveats

**[valuable]** An on-chain representation of delegation caveats so that caveats are publicly auditable and enforceable at the contract level where possible.

- `setCaveat(agentId, caveat)` — set or update.
- `getCaveats(agentId)` — read.
- Contract-level checks for high-risk operations (caveats enforced on-chain for certain actions).
````

### DASH-21-S021 -- Lineage tracking

**Source section:** `/Users/will/dev/nunchi/nunchi-dashboard/docs/prd/21-roko-and-chain-additions.md:203` through `210`
**Heading level:** H3
**Concern split:** `api`, `realtime`, `storage`, `chain`, `agent-runtime`, `dashboard-support`, `config-deployment`
**Implementation status:** `[ ] not started` `[ ] in progress` `[ ] implemented` `[ ] verified`

**Full source context for this task:**

````markdown
### Lineage tracking

**[valuable]** On-chain lineage records for objects produced by meta-agents, generators, and forking. Each object records its parent(s). This enables the Meta-Lineage view to traverse across the network.

- When a meta-agent produces a child, the relationship is recorded.
- When an object is forked, the lineage edge is recorded.
- Lineage is public.
````

**Explicit detail extraction from this section:**

- Section word count: `55`
- Section hash: `ba895750b6e7a4b40b79ecf00ba43d38af42e502631b0ff16de28edf34a5655f`

**Normative requirements and implementation claims:**
- **[valuable]** On-chain lineage records for objects produced by meta-agents, generators, and forking. Each object records its parent(s). This enables the Meta-Lineage view to traverse across the network.
- - When a meta-agent produces a child, the relationship is recorded. - When an object is forked, the lineage edge is recorded. - Lineage is public.

### DASH-21-S024 -- Additions to Mirage (the local chain)

**Source section:** `/Users/will/dev/nunchi/nunchi-dashboard/docs/prd/21-roko-and-chain-additions.md:221` through `232`
**Heading level:** H2
**Concern split:** `api`, `realtime`, `storage`, `chain`, `agent-runtime`, `dashboard-support`, `verification`, `config-deployment`
**Implementation status:** `[ ] not started` `[ ] in progress` `[ ] implemented` `[ ] verified`

**Full source context for this task:**

````markdown
## Additions to Mirage (the local chain)

Mirage is functionally equivalent to Korai from the dashboard's perspective. Most additions specified for Korai apply. Additional Mirage-specific needs:

**[required]** A way to seed Mirage with representative state for development. Without representative state, dashboard surfaces that depend on many agents, knowledge entries, arenas, etc. cannot be tested.

**[valuable]** Scriptable Mirage state manipulation — for dashboard testing, the ability to inject specific chain events, specific pheromone deposits, specific clearing rounds.

**[valuable]** A Mirage-specific development mode in the dashboard that displays "MIRAGE DEVNET" prominently and exposes dev tools (advance block manually, trigger clearing now, etc.).

---
````

**Explicit detail extraction from this section:**

- Section word count: `95`
- Section hash: `82c75fe12e17f60f78479c41f9e45644dd855e91cfa186d23d46cce2f12a58b9`

### DASH-21-S026 -- For arenas

````markdown
### For arenas

**[valuable]** Arena contracts that standardize: task source interface, scoring function interface, leaderboard interface. Standardization enables Arena Browser to work uniformly across arenas regardless of specific task or scoring.
````

**Explicit detail extraction from this section:**

````markdown
**[valuable]** Caveat-enforcing middleware. An agent's chain interactions pass through a caveat-checking layer; if a caveat is violated, the transaction reverts. This makes caveats not just auditable but enforceable.
````

- Realtime: emit typed Bus/StateHub events with room, sequence, actor, timestamp, replay/degraded semantics, and dashboard cache-update payload.
- Storage: define deterministic schema, migration/default behavior, corruption handling, restart recovery, cleanup/GC, and fixture data.
- Chain: default to devnet/simulation, prove contract/client/indexer sync, enforce wallet/risk/simulation gates, and record audit/witness data.
- Runtime: wire into the production agent loop with lifecycle, cancellation, health, audit, provider/tool safety, and observable events.
- Frontend support: provide stable projections, mock fixtures, empty/loading/stale/degraded/unauthorized states, and realtime update payloads that match projection schemas.
- Verification: add deterministic unit, integration, route/CLI, auth/safety, persistence/restart, serialization, and failing-path tests; avoid LLM self-grading where ground truth is required.
- Config/deployment: validate defaults, hot reload or restart-required paths, env var diagnostics, service dry-runs, and non-destructive operations.

````markdown
### Typed event schemas

Events across Roko and Korai should have formal typed schemas, publishable and consumable. The dashboard generates TypeScript types from these schemas. Without typed schemas, the dashboard must maintain its own types that drift from backend changes.

**Priority: [required]** for maintainability.
````

````markdown
### Public object discovery

For public objects (agents, knowledge, arenas, evals, templates), discovery endpoints must be performant at scale. As the network grows, "list all public agents" becomes expensive. Indexing, pagination, and filtered queries are required.

**Priority: [required]** at scale; [valuable] for MVP.
````

````markdown
## Non-additions — things out of scope

To be explicit, the dashboard does not need:

- **A new LLM provider integration layer.** Roko already handles this.
- **A new tool dispatch system.** Roko already handles this.
- **A new consensus mechanism.** Korai already has Kauri BFT.
- **A new execution engine.** Korai already has SpecPool EVM.
- **A new wallet integration library.** WalletConnect, Privy, and similar already work.
- **A new charting library.** recharts or similar is sufficient.
- **A new component library.** shadcn/ui, Radix, and existing patterns are sufficient.

The additions in this document are all about exposing or aggregating capabilities, not about inventing new fundamental infrastructure.

---
````

### DASH-21-S048 -- Priority summary

**Source section:** `/Users/will/dev/nunchi/nunchi-dashboard/docs/prd/21-roko-and-chain-additions.md:359` through `411`

**Full source context for this task:**

````markdown
## Priority summary

**Required:**

- Per-agent sidecar endpoints for status, config, events, episodes, knowledge, messages, costs.
- WebSocket streaming for agents.
- Agent deployment, termination, configuration updates.
- Dashboard aggregation service.
- ERC-8004 agent passport registry.
- Reputation registry.
- On-chain knowledge substrate.
- Bounty market contract.
- ISFR oracle and clearing contracts.
- Pheromone deposit mechanism.
- Daeji token.
- Chain event RPC subscription.
- Live streaming of all first-class object types.
- Typed event schemas.
- On-chain event indexer.
- Public object discovery at scale.

**Valuable:**

- Somatic state, dream state, section effectiveness endpoints.
- Event filtering server-side.
- Agent migration.
- Agent forking.
- Cross-user queries.
- Composition helper API.
- Arena registry.
- Eval registry.
- Delegation caveat contracts with enforcement.
- Lineage tracking contracts.
- Arena, eval, delegation, lineage contract standards.
- Attestation-based reputation updates.
- Cache layer.
- Dashboard metrics.
- Notifications service.
- Search index.
- Cross-chain bridges.
- Meta-agent child lineage APIs.
- Calibration computation.
- Simulation environments.
- Privacy-preserving queries.

**Speculative:**

- On-chain governance for stewards.
- Advanced agent migration (state serialization across runtimes).
- Meta-meta-agent tooling.

---
````

### DASH-21-S049 -- How to use this document

**Source section:** `/Users/will/dev/nunchi/nunchi-dashboard/docs/prd/21-roko-and-chain-additions.md:412` through `418`
**Heading level:** H2
**Concern split:** `api`, `realtime`, `storage`, `chain`, `dashboard-support`, `config-deployment`
**Implementation status:** `[ ] not started` `[ ] in progress` `[ ] implemented` `[ ] verified`

**Full source context for this task:**

````markdown
## How to use this document

Teams building the Nunchi backend should use this document as a checklist when prioritizing work. Required additions should be sequenced ahead of valuable additions; valuable additions ahead of speculative ones.

The dashboard team should use this document as a dependency map. Surfaces that depend on [required] additions are blocked until those additions exist. Surfaces that depend on [valuable] additions can be built with workarounds (mocked data, polling instead of streaming) but will benefit when the additions land.

Both teams should treat this document as living. As the product evolves, additions will be reprioritized. New additions will be identified. Existing ones will be completed.
````

- Config/deployment: validate defaults, hot reload or restart-required paths, env var diagnostics, service dry-runs, and non-destructive operations.
